# Hammer

# Description __

A Hammer, used to upgrade building materials. Right-click for the options. You can also pick up deployed objects while the hammer is equipped.

Page views: 5,854  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Salvaged Hammer

# Description __

A Hammer made from a bunch of other crap. Yields the same amount of ore and wood as the stone hatchet and stone pickaxe.

Page views: 5,947  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Candle Hat

# Description __

A hat with a candle on top. You can turn the candle on in your inventory.

Page views: 2,962  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Miners Hat

# Description __

A leather cap with a flashlight attached. It uses Low Grade Fuel and can be activated from the inventory.

Page views: 2,861  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Wolf Headdress

# Description __

A headdress made out of the scraped out head of a wolf.

# Stats __

Damage Type | Percentage  
---|---  
Projectile | 30 %  
Melee | 60 %  
Bite | 10 %  
Radiation | 4 %  
Cold | 6 %  
Explosion | 13 %  
  
Page views: 3,804  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Description __

A hazmat suit made from radiation resistant rubber.

# Arctic Scientist Suit

# Description __

A hazmat suit made from radiation resistant rubber.

Page views: 4,157  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/heavy.plate.helmet~history)



# Heavy Plate Helmet

# Description __

Offers superior protection at the cost of reduced vision and movement speed.

Page views: 3,641  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Heavy Plate Jacket

# Description __

Offers superior protection at the cost of aiming down sights and reduced movement speed.

Page views: 3,179  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/hitchtroughcombo~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/hitchtroughcombo~history)



# Hitch & Trough

# Description __

A Hitching post and Trough. Dismounting your horses here will keep them healthy and fed as long as it is kept stocked with food.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x200 Wood



## Recycling Output __

  * x100 Wood



Page views: 10,632  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Hoodie

# Description __

A hoodie.

# Stats __

Damage Type | Percentage  
---|---  
Projectile | 15 %  
Melee | 15 %  
Bite | 6 %  
Radiation | 5 %  
Cold | 8 %  
  
# Loot Rates __

Container | Chance  
---|---  
Supply Drop | 12 %  
Tool Box | 3 %  
Locked Crate | 3 %  
Sunken Crate | 2 %  
Elite Tier Crate | 1 %  
Military Crate | 1 %  
Oil Rig Scientist | 0.1 %  
Heavy Scientist | 0.1 %  
  
Item does not stack and its despawn time is 20 min.

Page views: 3,446  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Roadsign Horse Armor

# Description __

A set of roadsign armor for a horse

Riding a horse with equipped armor will reduce the amount of damage dealt to the rider.

Page views: 3,076  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Wooden Horse Armor

# Description __

A set of wooden horse armor

Riding a horse with equipped armor will reduce the amount of damage dealt to the rider.

Page views: 3,116  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Saddle bag

# Description __

Equipping this saddle bag will add extra storage space on your horse

You can equip up to two Saddle Bags in a horse, by doing it you will increase 6 slots in its inventory for each Saddle Bag equipped. Horse's speed will be slowed by -3.6 km/h for each Saddle Bag equipped.

Item does not stack and its despawn time is 5 min.

Page views: 5,569  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Cooked Horse Meat

# Description __

Cooked Horse Meat. Eating it will restore some health, hunger, and thirst.

Page views: 2,084  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Raw Horse Meat

# Description __

Raw Horse Meat. Eating it will damage your health, try cooking it first.

Page views: 3,708  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [High Quality Metal Ore](/rust/item/hq.metal.ore)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/hq.metal.ore)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/hq.metal.ore~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/hq.metal.ore~history)



# High Quality Metal Ore

# Description __

A rock containing High Quality Metal. Can be smelted in a furnace.

# Obtaining __

You can find HQM Ore by mining metal nodes to completion. On the finishing blow of a metal ore node, you get 2 HQM ore. On its own, HQM Ore is useless. You will need a [small](/rust/item/furnace) or [large furnace](/rust/item/furnace.large) to smelth it down into [High Quality Metal (HQM)](/rust/item/metal.refined). From there, you can use it to upgrade your base to the strongest material or craft some T3 guns, like the [AK-47](/rust/item/rifle.ak).

It can also be found in red barrels along roads and monuments.

Page views: 3,536  
Updated: This Year

# Burnt Human Meat

# Description __

Burned Meat from a human being. Consuming will damage your health.

Page views: 2,148  
Updated: A Long Time Ago
